;v{kzadvitIyam}

fkzo mahIDare cApi BallUke SoRake'pi ca ..
;l{0005}
kftaveDe vAcyaliNgaM nakzatre tu napuMsakam .

spardDApade ca dormUle kacCavIruttfRe'pi ca .
kakzo'mrAhiRikA'kAYcIprakozWagajarajjuzu ..
raTaBAge'pi kANkzyaH syAdvIkzyavismayadfSyayoH .
;l{0010}

utprekzA'navaDAne'pi kAvyAlaNkaraRAntare .
